# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
An increasing function is one whose gradient is always at least 0.




It would be "strictly increasing" if f(x) > 0 for all x, i.e it is not allowed to go horizontal. ^PwDRG6gl

Show that the function


is increasing for all real values of x ^OwSCpTPY

Find the interval on which the function f(x) = 
is decreasing ^AVRtejFX

Lagrange's ^twuLUBY5

Leibniz's ^Hzy1BP1i

Newton's ^vLocOZ1u
